    SELECT TOP(2) [p].[id], [p].[birth_date], [p].[expose_data], [p].[can_receive_message], [p].[cpf], [p].[created_at], [p].[email], [p].[name], [p].[perfil_image_src], [p].[person_type], [p].[phone_number], [p].[updated_at], [e].[id] AS [id0], [e].[created_at] AS [created_at0], [e].[end_date], [e].[enterprise], [e].[is_public], [e].[is_public_initiative], [e].[person_id], [e].[role], [e].[salary_range], [e].[start_date], [e].[updated_at] AS [updated_at0], [a].[id] AS [id1], [a].[country], [a].[created_at] AS [created_at1], [a].[is_public] AS [is_public0], [a].[person_id] AS [person_id0], [a].[state], [a].[updated_at] AS [updated_at1], [c].[id] AS [id2], [c].[created_at] AS [created_at2], [c].[has_certification], [c].[has_doctorate_degree], [c].[has_master_degree], [c].[has_specialization], [c].[is_public] AS [is_public1], [c].[person_id] AS [person_id1], [c].[updated_at] AS [updated_at2]
    FROM [Person] AS [p]
    LEFT JOIN [Employment] AS [e] ON [p].[id] = [e].[person_id]
    LEFT JOIN [Address] AS [a] ON [p].[id] = [a].[person_id]
    LEFT JOIN [ContinuingEducation] AS [c] ON [p].[id] = [c].[person_id]
    WHERE [p].[id] = @__id_0
) AS [t]
LEFT JOIN (
    SELECT [p0].[id], [p0].[beginning_semester], [p0].[course_id], [p0].[created_at], [p0].[final_semester], [p0].[level], [p0].[mat], [p0].[modality], [p0].[person_id], [p0].[updated_at], [c0].[id] AS [id0], [c0].[course_name], [c0].[created_at] AS [created_at0], [c0].[normalized_course_name], [c0].[updated_at] AS [updated_at0]
    FROM [PersonCourse] AS [p0]
    INNER JOIN [Course] AS [c0] ON [p0].[course_id] = [c0].[id]
) AS [t0] ON [t].[id] = [t0].[person_id]
LEFT JOIN [Highlights] AS [h] ON [t].[id] = [h].[person_id]
LEFT JOIN [Testimony] AS [t1] ON [t].[id] = [t1].[person_id]
ORDER BY [t].[id], [t].[id0], [t].[id1], [t].[id2], [t0].[id], [t0].[id0], [h].[id]

    SELECT TOP(2) [p].[id], [p].[birth_date], [p].[expose_data], [p].[can_receive_message], [p].[cpf], [p].[created_at], [p].[email], [p].[name], [p].[perfil_image_src], [p].[person_type], [p].[phone_number], [p].[updated_at], [e].[id] AS [id0], [e].[created_at] AS [created_at0], [e].[end_date], [e].[enterprise], [e].[is_public], [e].[is_public_initiative], [e].[person_id], [e].[role], [e].[salary_range], [e].[start_date], [e].[updated_at] AS [updated_at0], [a].[id] AS [id1], [a].[country], [a].[created_at] AS [created_at1], [a].[is_public] AS [is_public0], [a].[person_id] AS [person_id0], [a].[state], [a].[updated_at] AS [updated_at1], [c].[id] AS [id2], [c].[created_at] AS [created_at2], [c].[has_certification], [c].[has_doctorate_degree], [c].[has_master_degree], [c].[has_specialization], [c].[is_public] AS [is_public1], [c].[person_id] AS [person_id1], [c].[updated_at] AS [updated_at2]
    FROM [Person] AS [p]
    LEFT JOIN [Employment] AS [e] ON [p].[id] = [e].[person_id]
    LEFT JOIN [Address] AS [a] ON [p].[id] = [a].[person_id]
    LEFT JOIN [ContinuingEducation] AS [c] ON [p].[id] = [c].[person_id]
    WHERE [p].[id] = @__id_0
) AS [t]
LEFT JOIN (
    SELECT [p0].[id], [p0].[beginning_semester], [p0].[course_id], [p0].[created_at], [p0].[final_semester], [p0].[level], [p0].[mat], [p0].[modality], [p0].[person_id], [p0].[updated_at], [c0].[id] AS [id0], [c0].[course_name], [c0].[created_at] AS [created_at0], [c0].[normalized_course_name], [c0].[updated_at] AS [updated_at0]
    FROM [PersonCourse] AS [p0]
    INNER JOIN [Course] AS [c0] ON [p0].[course_id] = [c0].[id]
) AS [t0] ON [t].[id] = [t0].[person_id]
LEFT JOIN [Highlights] AS [h] ON [t].[id] = [h].[person_id]
LEFT JOIN [Testimony] AS [t1] ON [t].[id] = [t1].[person_id]
ORDER BY [t].[id], [t].[id0], [t].[id1], [t].[id2], [t0].[id], [t0].[id0], [h].[id]

    SELECT TOP(2) [p].[id], [p].[birth_date], [p].[expose_data], [p].[can_receive_message], [p].[cpf], [p].[created_at], [p].[email], [p].[name], [p].[perfil_image_src], [p].[person_type], [p].[phone_number], [p].[updated_at], [e].[id] AS [id0], [e].[created_at] AS [created_at0], [e].[end_date], [e].[enterprise], [e].[is_public], [e].[is_public_initiative], [e].[person_id], [e].[role], [e].[salary_range], [e].[start_date], [e].[updated_at] AS [updated_at0], [a].[id] AS [id1], [a].[country], [a].[created_at] AS [created_at1], [a].[is_public] AS [is_public0], [a].[person_id] AS [person_id0], [a].[state], [a].[updated_at] AS [updated_at1], [c].[id] AS [id2], [c].[created_at] AS [created_at2], [c].[has_certification], [c].[has_doctorate_degree], [c].[has_master_degree], [c].[has_specialization], [c].[is_public] AS [is_public1], [c].[person_id] AS [person_id1], [c].[updated_at] AS [updated_at2]
    FROM [Person] AS [p]
    LEFT JOIN [Employment] AS [e] ON [p].[id] = [e].[person_id]
    LEFT JOIN [Address] AS [a] ON [p].[id] = [a].[person_id]
    LEFT JOIN [ContinuingEducation] AS [c] ON [p].[id] = [c].[person_id]
    WHERE [p].[id] = @__id_0
) AS [t]
LEFT JOIN (
    SELECT [p0].[id], [p0].[beginning_semester], [p0].[course_id], [p0].[created_at], [p0].[final_semester], [p0].[level], [p0].[mat], [p0].[modality], [p0].[person_id], [p0].[updated_at], [c0].[id] AS [id0], [c0].[course_name], [c0].[created_at] AS [created_at0], [c0].[normalized_course_name], [c0].[updated_at] AS [updated_at0]

ORDER BY [t].[id], [t].[id0], [t].[id1], [t].[id2], [t0].[id], [t0].[id0], [h].[id]

    SELECT TOP(2) [p].[id], [p].[birth_date], [p].[expose_data], [p].[can_receive_message], [p].[cpf], [p].[created_at], [p].[email], [p].[name], [p].[perfil_image_src], [p].[person_type], [p].[phone_number], [p].[updated_at], [e].[id] AS [id0], [e].[created_at] AS [created_at0], [e].[end_date], [e].[enterprise], [e].[is_public], [e].[is_public_initiative], [e].[person_id], [e].[role], [e].[salary_range], [e].[start_date], [e].[updated_at] AS [updated_at0], [a].[id] AS [id1], [a].[country], [a].[created_at] AS [created_at1], [a].[is_public] AS [is_public0], [a].[person_id] AS [person_id0], [a].[state], [a].[updated_at] AS [updated_at1], [c].[id] AS [id2], [c].[created_at] AS [created_at2], [c].[has_certification], [c].[has_doctorate_degree], [c].[has_master_degree], [c].[has_specialization], [c].[is_public] AS [is_public1], [c].[person_id] AS [person_id1], [c].[updated_at] AS [updated_at2]
    FROM [Person] AS [p]
    LEFT JOIN [Employment] AS [e] ON [p].[id] = [e].[person_id]
    LEFT JOIN [Address] AS [a] ON [p].[id] = [a].[person_id]
    LEFT JOIN [ContinuingEducation] AS [c] ON [p].[id] = [c].[person_id]
    WHERE [p].[id] = @__id_0
) AS [t]
LEFT JOIN (
    SELECT [p0].[id], [p0].[beginning_semester], [p0].[course_id], [p0].[created_at], [p0].[final_semester], [p0].[level], [p0].[mat], [p0].[modality], [p0].[person_id], [p0].[updated_at], [c0].[id] AS [id0], [c0].[course_name], [c0].[created_at] AS [created_at0], [c0].[normalized_course_name], [c0].[updated_at] AS [updated_at0]
    FROM [PersonCourse] AS [p0]
    INNER JOIN [Course] AS [c0] ON [p0].[course_id] = [c0].[id]
) AS [t0] ON [t].[id] = [t0].[person_id]
LEFT JOIN [Highlights] AS [h] ON [t].[id] = [h].[person_id]
LEFT JOIN [Testimony] AS [t1] ON [t].[id] = [t1].[person_id]
ORDER BY [t].[id], [t].[id0], [t].[id1], [t].[id2], [t0].[id], [t0].[id0], [h].[id]

    SELECT TOP(2) [p].[id], [p].[birth_date], [p].[expose_data], [p].[can_receive_message], [p].[cpf], [p].[created_at], [p].[email], [p].[name], [p].[perfil_image_src], [p].[person_type], [p].[phone_number], [p].[updated_at], [e].[id] AS [id0], [e].[created_at] AS [created_at0], [e].[end_date], [e].[enterprise], [e].[is_public], [e].[is_public_initiative], [e].[person_id], [e].[role], [e].[salary_range], [e].[start_date], [e].[updated_at] AS [updated_at0], [a].[id] AS [id1], [a].[country], [a].[created_at] AS [created_at1], [a].[is_public] AS [is_public0], [a].[person_id] AS [person_id0], [a].[state], [a].[updated_at] AS [updated_at1], [c].[id] AS [id2], [c].[created_at] AS [created_at2], [c].[has_certification], [c].[has_doctorate_degree], [c].[has_master_degree], [c].[has_specialization], [c].[is_public] AS [is_public1], [c].[person_id] AS [person_id1], [c].[updated_at] AS [updated_at2]
    FROM [Person] AS [p]
    LEFT JOIN [Employment] AS [e] ON [p].[id] = [e].[person_id]
    LEFT JOIN [Address] AS [a] ON [p].[id] = [a].[person_id]
    LEFT JOIN [ContinuingEducation] AS [c] ON [p].[id] = [c].[person_id]
    WHERE [p].[id] = @__id_0
) AS [t]
LEFT JOIN (
    SELECT [p0].[id], [p0].[beginning_semester], [p0].[course_id], [p0].[created_at], [p0].[final_semester], [p0].[level], [p0].[mat], [p0].[modality], [p0].[person_id], [p0].[updated_at], [c0].[id] AS [id0], [c0].[course_name], [c0].[created_at] AS [created_at0], [c0].[normalized_course_name], [c0].[updated_at] AS [updated_at0]
    FROM [PersonCourse] AS [p0]
    INNER JOIN [Course] AS [c0] ON [p0].[course_id] = [c0].[id]
) AS [t0] ON [t].[id] = [t0].[person_id]
LEFT JOIN [Highlights] AS [h] ON [t].[id] = [h].[person_id]
LEFT JOIN [Testimony] AS [t1] ON [t].[id] = [t1].[person_id]
ORDER BY [t].[id], [t].[id0], [t].[id1], [t].[id2], [t0].[id], [t0].[id0], [h].[id]

    SELECT TOP(2) [p].[id], [p].[birth_date], [p].[expose_data], [p].[can_receive_message], [p].[cpf], [p].[created_at], [p].[email], [p].[name], [p].[perfil_image_src], [p].[person_type], [p].[phone_number], [p].[updated_at], [e].[id] AS [id0], [e].[created_at] AS [created_at0], [e].[end_date], [e].[enterprise], [e].[is_public], [e].[is_public_initiative], [e].[person_id], [e].[role], [e].[salary_range], [e].[start_date], [e].[updated_at] AS [updated_at0], [a].[id] AS [id1], [a].[country], [a].[created_at] AS [created_at1], [a].[is_public] AS [is_public0], [a].[person_id] AS [person_id0], [a].[state], [a].[updated_at] AS [updated_at1], [c].[id] AS [id2], [c].[created_at] AS [created_at2], [c].[has_certification], [c].[has_doctorate_degree], [c].[has_master_degree], [c].[has_specialization], [c].[is_public] AS [is_public1], [c].[person_id] AS [person_id1], [c].[updated_at] AS [updated_at2]
    FROM [Person] AS [p]
    LEFT JOIN [Employment] AS [e] ON [p].[id] = [e].[person_id]
    LEFT JOIN [Address] AS [a] ON [p].[id] = [a].[person_id]
    LEFT JOIN [ContinuingEducation] AS [c] ON [p].[id] = [c].[person_id]
    WHERE [p].[id] = @__id_0
) AS [t]
LEFT JOIN (
    SELECT [p0].[id], [p0].[beginning_semester], [p0].[course_id], [p0].[created_at], [p0].[final_semester], [p0].[level], [p0].[mat], [p0].[modality], [p0].[person_id], [p0].[updated_at], [c0].[id] AS [id0], [c0].[course_name], [c0].[created_at] AS [created_at0], [c0].[normalized_course_name], [c0].[updated_at] AS [updated_at0]
    FROM [PersonCourse] AS [p0]
    INNER JOIN [Course] AS [c0] ON [p0].[course_id] = [c0].[id]
) AS [t0] ON [t].[id] = [t0].[person_id]
LEFT JOIN [Highlights] AS [h] ON [t].[id] = [h].[person_id]
LEFT JOIN [Testimony] AS [t1] ON [t].[id] = [t1].[person_id]
ORDER BY [t].[id], [t].[id0], [t].[id1], [t].[id2], [t0].[id], [t0].[id0], [h].[id]

    SELECT TOP(2) [p].[id], [p].[birth_date], [p].[expose_data], [p].[can_receive_message], [p].[cpf], [p].[created_at], [p].[email], [p].[name], [p].[perfil_image_src], [p].[person_type], [p].[phone_number], [p].[updated_at], [e].[id] AS [id0], [e].[created_at] AS [created_at0], [e].[end_date], [e].[enterprise], [e].[is_public], [e].[is_public_initiative], [e].[person_id], [e].[role], [e].[salary_range], [e].[start_date], [e].[updated_at] AS [updated_at0], [a].[id] AS [id1], [a].[country], [a].[created_at] AS [created_at1], [a].[is_public] AS [is_public0], [a].[person_id] AS [person_id0], [a].[state], [a].[updated_at] AS [updated_at1], [c].[id] AS [id2], [c].[created_at] AS [created_at2], [c].[has_certification], [c].[has_doctorate_degree], [c].[has_master_degree], [c].[has_specialization], [c].[is_public] AS [is_public1], [c].[person_id] AS [person_id1], [c].[updated_at] AS [updated_at2]
    FROM [Person] AS [p]
    LEFT JOIN [Employment] AS [e] ON [p].[id] = [e].[person_id]
    LEFT JOIN [Address] AS [a] ON [p].[id] = [a].[person_id]
    LEFT JOIN [ContinuingEducation] AS [c] ON [p].[id] = [c].[person_id]
    WHERE [p].[id] = @__id_0
) AS [t]
LEFT JOIN (
    SELECT [p0].[id], [p0].[beginning_semester], [p0].[course_id], [p0].[created_at], [p0].[final_semester], [p0].[level], [p0].[mat], [p0].[modality], [p0].[person_id], [p0].[updated_at], [c0].[id] AS [id0], [c0].[course_name], [c0].[created_at] AS [created_at0], [c0].[normalized_course_name], [c0].[updated_at] AS [updated_at0]
    FROM [PersonCourse] AS [p0]
    INNER JOIN [Course] AS [c0] ON [p0].[course_id] = [c0].[id]
) AS [t0] ON [t].[id] = [t0].[person_id]
LEFT JOIN [Highlights] AS [h] ON [t].[id] = [h].[person_id]
LEFT JOIN [Testimony] AS [t1] ON [t].[id] = [t1].[person_id]
ORDER BY [t].[id], [t].[id0], [t].[id1], [t].[id2], [t0].[id], [t0].[id0], [h].[id]

    SELECT [p0].[id], [p0].[beginning_semester], [p0].[course_id], [p0].[created_at], [p0].[final_semester], [p0].[level], [p0].[mat], [p0].[modality], [p0].[person_id], [p0].[updated_at], [c].[id] AS [id0], [c].[course_name], [c].[created_at] AS [created_at0], [c].[normalized_course_name], [c].[updated_at] AS [updated_at0]

) AS [t1] ON [p].[id] = [t1].[person_id]
WHERE [t].[was_accepted] = CAST(1 AS bit)
